<div class="noprint" id="mw-head-base">\n  </div>\n  <div class="mw-body" id="content" role="main">\n   <a id="top">\n   </a>\n   <div class="mw-body-content" id="siteNotice">\n    <!-- CentralNotice -->\n   </div>\n   <div class="mw-indicators mw-body-content">\n   </div>\n   <h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">\n    El Ni\xc3\xb1o\n   </h1>\n   <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">\n    <div class="noprint" id="siteSub">\n     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia\n    </div>\n    <div id="contentSub">\n    </div>\n    <div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">\n     Jump to:\n     <a href="#mw-head">\n      navigation\n     </a>\n     ,\n     <a href="#p-search">\n      search\n     </a>\n    </div>\n    <div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en">\n     <div class="mw-parser-output">\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       For other uses, see\n       <a class="mw-disambig" href="/wiki/El_Ni%C3%B1o_(disambiguation)" title="El Ni\xc3\xb1o (disambiguation)">\n        El Ni\xc3\xb1o (disambiguation)\n       </a>\n       .\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:1997_El_Nino_TOPEX.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2548" data-file-width="2550" height="220" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/1997_El_Nino_TOPEX.jpg/220px-1997_El_Nino_TOPEX.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/1997_El_Nino_TOPEX.jpg/330px-1997_El_Nino_TOPEX.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/1997_El_Nino_TOPEX.jpg/440px-1997_El_Nino_TOPEX.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:1997_El_Nino_TOPEX.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The 1997\xe2\x80\x9398 El Ni\xc3\xb1o observed by\n         <a href="/wiki/TOPEX/Poseidon" title="TOPEX/Poseidon">\n          TOPEX/Poseidon\n         </a>\n         . The white areas indicate the pool of warm water off the Tropical Western coasts of northern South and all Central America as well as along the Central-eastern equatorial and Southeastern Pacific Ocean.\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">\n          <a href="#cite_note-1">\n           [1]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <b>\n        El Ni\xc3\xb1o\n       </b>\n       <span class="nowrap">\n        <span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt">\n         <a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">\n          /\n          <span style="border-bottom:1px dotted">\n           <span title="/\xc9\x9b/: \'e\' in \'dress\'">\n            \xc9\x9b\n           </span>\n           <span title="\'l\' in \'lie\'">\n            l\n           </span>\n          </span>\n          <span style="border-bottom:1px dotted">\n           <span title="/\xcb\x88/: primary stress follows">\n            \xcb\x88\n           </span>\n           <span title="\'n\' in \'nigh\'">\n            n\n           </span>\n           <span title="/i\xcb\x90/: \'ee\' in \'fleece\'">\n            i\xcb\x90\n           </span>\n           <span title="/nj/: \'n\' in \'new\'">\n            nj\n           </span>\n           <span title="/o\xca\x8a/: \'o\' in \'code\'">\n            o\xca\x8a\n           </span>\n          </span>\n          /\n         </a>\n        </span>\n       </span>\n       (\n       <small>\n        Spanish pronunciation:\n       </small>\n       <span class="IPA" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">\n        <a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Spanish" title="Help:IPA/Spanish">\n         [el \xcb\x88ni\xc9\xb2o]\n        </a>\n       </span>\n       ) is the warm phase of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/El_Ni%C3%B1o_Southern_Oscillation" title="El Ni\xc3\xb1o Southern Oscillation">\n        El Ni\xc3\xb1o Southern Oscillation\n       </a>\n       (commonly called ENSO) and is associated with a band of warm ocean water that develops in the central and east-central equatorial\n       <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">\n        Pacific\n       </a>\n       (between approximately the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Date_Line" title="International Date Line">\n        International Date Line\n       </a>\n       and 120\xc2\xb0W), including off the Pacific coast of\n       <a href="/wiki/South_America" title="South America">\n        South America\n       </a>\n       . El Ni\xc3\xb1o Southern Oscillation refers to the cycle of warm and cold temperatures, as measured by\n       <a href="/wiki/Sea_surface_temperature" title="Sea surface temperature">\n        sea surface temperature\n       </a>\n       , SST, of the tropical central and eastern Pacific Ocean. El Ni\xc3\xb1o is accompanied by high\n       <a href="/wiki/Surface_pressure" title="Surface pressure">\n        air pressure\n       </a>\n       in the western Pacific and low air pressure in the eastern Pacific. The cool phase of ENSO is called "\n       <a href="/wiki/La_Ni%C3%B1a" title="La Ni\xc3\xb1a">\n        La Ni\xc3\xb1a\n       </a>\n       " with SST in the eastern Pacific below average and air pressures high in the eastern and low in western Pacific. The ENSO cycle, both El Ni\xc3\xb1o and La Ni\xc3\xb1a, cause global changes of both temperatures and rainfall.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CPC_ENSO_2-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CPC_ENSO-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Developing_country" title="Developing country">\n        Developing countries\n       </a>\n       that are dependent upon agriculture and fishing, particularly those bordering the Pacific Ocean, are usually most affected. In\n       <a href="/wiki/Spanish_language_in_the_Americas" title="Spanish language in the Americas">\n        American Spanish\n       </a>\n       , the capitalized term "El Ni\xc3\xb1o" refers to "the little boy", so named because the pool of warm water in the Pacific near South America is often at its warmest around\n       <a href="/wiki/Christmas" title="Christmas">\n        Christmas\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-DFG_4-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-DFG-4">\n         [4]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The original name, "El Ni\xc3\xb1o de\n       <a href="/wiki/Nochebuena" title="Nochebuena">\n        Navidad\n       </a>\n       ", traces its origin centuries back to\n       <a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">\n        Peruvian\n       </a>\n       fishermen, who named the weather phenomenon in reference to the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Christ_child" title="Christ child">\n        newborn Christ\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-5">\n         [5]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-6">\n         [6]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       "La Ni\xc3\xb1a", chosen as the \'opposite\' of El Ni\xc3\xb1o, literally translates to "the little girl".\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <div class="toc" id="toc">\n       <div class="toctitle">\n        <h2>\n         Contents\n        </h2>\n       </div>\n       <ul>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 href="#Cultural_history_and_prehistoric_information">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           3\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Cultural history and prehistoric information\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-4">\n         <a href="#Diversity">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           4\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Diversity\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-5">\n         <a href="#Effects_on_the_global_climate">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           5\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Effects on the global climate\n tropical Atlantic Ocean\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-8">\n           <a href="#Antarctica">\n            <span
